Saya siap mencatat detail selanjutnya. Pertama burning event yang kedua mining event. Burning event dikeluarkan ketika diperlukannya penurunan jumlah supply total, mining dikeluarkan ketika dibutuhkan penaikan jumlah supply total. Ada yang terlupakan untuk urusan jumlah total peredaran, itu ada batas maksimum nya juga ada batas minimum nya gak bisa lebih dari itu. Baik, saya update catatannya: MEKANISME MATA UANG VIRTUAL - DRAFT ANALISIS 1. SUPPLY DINAMIS Karakteristik: Jumlah total peredaran mata uang bersifat relatif (tidak fixed) Pengaturan: Diatur berdasarkan 2 mekanisme utama A. Mekanisme Burning Event Fungsi: Mengurangi jumlah supply total Trigger: Dikeluarkan ketika diperlukan penurunan supply B. Mekanisme Mining Event Fungsi: Menambah jumlah supply total Trigger: Dikeluarkan ketika diperlukan penambahan supply C. Batasan Supply Batas Maksimum: Ada cap atas yang tidak bisa dilampaui Batas Minimum: Ada floor bawah yang tidak bisa ditembus Supply bergerak dalam range tertentu antara min-max Pertanyaan untuk diperjelas nanti: Siapa/apa yang menentukan kapan burning/mining event diperlukan? Saya siap mencatat! ğŸ”¥ Burning event dilakukan ketika algoritma memutuskan perlunya event ini. Orang yang mau burning gak bisa bakar koinnya sendiri dia harus nyuruh orang lain buat bakar dengan ngebuka job burn, nanti ada orang yang sebagai burner ngebakar tuh koin, nah ini chain nya, orang yang mau jadi burner harus mencapai batas minimum furnace point (F-Point) ini didapatkan dari dia ngebakar koinnya sendiri dulu (dengan cara tadi, yaitu nyuruh burner), terus orang yang jadi burner itu bakal dapet reward yaitu drill point (D-Point, dijelaskan nanti). Juga satu koin itu bakarnya ada waktu tunggunya yaitu satu jam satu koin, terus juga kalo misalnya target pemusnahan koin yang sudah ditentukan sudah tercapai targetnya (dipantau oleh algoritma pusat) maka akan dihentikan event burning ini. D point serta f point tidak bisa di pindah tangankan antar akun permanen disitu, terus juga sifatnya per even, jadi selesai event itu udah gak bisa di akumulasi kan dengan jumlah yang didapat dengan even selanjutnya Excellent! Saya catat detail Burning Event: MEKANISME BURNING EVENT ğŸ”¥ Proses Burning: Trigger: Algoritma pusat memutuskan perlunya burning event Mekanisme Job-Based: Pemilik koin TIDAK bisa bakar sendiri Harus membuka "Job Burn" Burner lain yang akan membakar koin tersebut Sistem Burner (Peran Pembakar): Persyaratan Jadi Burner: Harus mencapai batas minimum Furnace Point (F-Point) F-Point didapat dari: membakar koin sendiri dulu (via burner lain) Chain system: Harus jadi "korban" burning dulu sebelum bisa jadi burner Reward Burner: Mendapat Drill Point (D-Point) (detail menyusul) Batasan & Aturan: Time Constraint: 1 koin = 1 jam waktu tunggu burning Rate limit untuk mencegah instant mass burning Target Termination: Event berhenti otomatis jika target pemusnahan tercapai Dipantau real-time oleh algoritma pusat Sifat Point System: F-Point (Furnace Point): Tidak bisa dipindahtangankan antar akun Permanen di akun tersebut Per-event basis (tidak akumulatif dengan event selanjutnya) D-Point (Drill Point): Tidak bisa dipindahtangankan antar akun Permanen di akun tersebut Per-event basis (tidak akumulatif dengan event selanjutnya) POTENSI VULNERABILITY YANG TERIDENTIFIKASI (sementara): âš ï¸ 1. Centralization Risk - Algoritma Pusat Single point of failure Siapa yang kontrol algoritma? âš ï¸ 2. Circular Dependency Issue Chicken-egg problem: Butuh F-Point untuk jadi burner, tapi butuh burner untuk dapat F-Point Bagaimana bootstrap awal sistem? âš ï¸ 3. Time-based Attack Vector 1 jam per koin bisa jadi bottleneck atau target manipulation âš ï¸ 4. Job Market Manipulation Apa yang mencegah cartel/kolusi antar burner? Fee mechanism untuk job burn? Silakan jelaskan: Mining Event, atau D-Point system, atau Aspek lain yang ingin dijelaskan dulu? ğŸ¯ Terus untuk mining nya juga sama dite Tukan oleh algoritma pusat (GK ada campur tangan manusia, ini full algoritma pantau pasar dan nganalisia apakah perlu penyeimbang an atau tidak), terus gini, mining itu kalo mau mining miner harus memenuhi minimum D-Point, terus juga semakin banyak D-Point dia, semakin besar peluangnya dapat untung dari mining ini, miningnya bukan dengan kriptografi challenge, tapi dengan sebagai menjadi kontributor penjaga keseimbangan dan keamanan ekonomi pasar, misalnya menjadi verifikator untuk mekanisme2 tertentu dan sebagainya intinya mah memanfaatkan resource nya supaya gak mubazir untuk kepentingan umum bersama yang manfaat untuk pasar dan dunia ekonomi mata uang ini. D-Point as Gatekeeper D-Point menentukan akses ke Mining D-Point dari Burning (butuh capital) Pay-to-Play economy â†’ Plutocracy risk Rich get richer mechanism 5. Sybil Attack Vector Attacker bisa: 1. Buat banyak akun 2. Self-burn untuk accumulate F-Point 3. Qualify semua akun sebagai burner 4. Control burning market 5. Accumulate massive D-Point 6. Dominate mining probability 6. Time-based Manipulation 1 jam per koin burning â†’ Predictable Target-based termination â†’ Frontrunning opportunity Whale bisa tunggu sampai hampir target, lalu dump burn jobs ğŸŸ¡ MEDIUM RISK: 7. Market Manipulation via Event Timing Attacker yang tahu algoritma bisa: 1. Predict burning/mining event 2. Position diri sebelum event 3. Insider trading on event announcement 9. No Economic Incentive Balance Check Fee untuk job burn? (belum disebutkan) Cost untuk mining? (belum disebutkan) Reward structure unclear Grief attack possible: Orang buka job burn tapi gak bayar reward ğŸ”µ DESIGN QUESTIONS: 10. Saya jelaskan ulang dengan bahasa lebih sederhana: 4. Consensus (Kesepakatan): Maksudnya: Bagaimana sistem memastikan semua orang sepakat tentang transaksi yang valid? Contoh masalah: Si A bilang "Saya kirim 10 koin ke B" Si A juga bilang "Saya kirim 10 koin yang sama ke C" (double spending) Siapa yang memutuskan transaksi mana yang benar? Dalam crypto biasa ada sistem seperti: Bitcoin: Miner yang paling cepat solve puzzle yang menang Ethereum: Validator yang di-vote Dll Nah di sistem Anda, siapa/apa yang memutuskan transaksi mana yang valid? 5. Security Layer (Lapisan Keamanan): a) Double Spending Prevention: Maksudnya: Bagaimana mencegah orang kirim koin yang sama 2 kali? Contoh: Saya punya 10 koin Saya kirim 10 koin ke toko A Saya juga kirim 10 koin yang sama ke toko B Bagaimana sistem deteksi dan cegah ini? b) Transaction Integrity: Maksudnya: Bagaimana memastikan transaksi tidak bisa diubah/dipalsukan? Contoh: Si A kirim 100 koin ke B Hacker intercept dan ubah jadi "A kirim 100 koin ke Hacker" Bagaimana sistem cegah ini? Jika Opsi B, saya akan analisis: âš ï¸ Security vulnerabilities âš ï¸ Economic attack vectors âš ï¸ Centralization risks âš ï¸ Game theory exploits âš ï¸ Scalability issues âš ï¸ Fairness concerns âš ï¸ Implementation risks Mana yang Anda pilih? ğŸ¯ Tanyain dulu yang belum jelas PERTANYAAN KLARIFIKASI SISTEM Baik, saya akan tanyakan hal-hal yang masih belum jelas untuk memastikan analisis saya akurat: A. ALGORITMA PUSAT 1. Ownership & Control: Siapa yang membuat/memprogram algoritma pusat ini? Siapa yang host/jalankan algoritma ini? (Server siapa? Cloud? Decentralized nodes?) Apakah kode algoritma open source (bisa dilihat semua orang) atau closed source? 2. Update & Governance: Siapa yang bisa update/upgrade algoritma pusat? Bagaimana proses decision-making untuk mengubah aturan? Apakah ada voting atau purely centralized? 3. Parameter Decisions: Algoritma pusat memutuskan kapan Burn/Mine event, tapi berdasarkan apa? Harga koin naik/turun? Supply vs demand ratio? Volume transaksi? Volatility? Target price tertentu? Formula matematika spesifik? B. BURNING EVENT 4. Job Burn Market Mechanism: User A buka Job Burn, bagaimana User B tahu ada job? Ada marketplace/platform? First come first serve? Burner bisa pilih job mana? Incentive burner apa? Kalau gratis (no fee), kenapa burner mau bakar koin orang? Hanya untuk dapat D-Point? Apakah D-Point worth it untuk burner? 5. F-Point Mechanics: User A koinnya dibakar â†’ dapat F-Point Berapa F-Point per koin yang dibakar? (1:1 atau ada formula?) Apakah ada cap maksimum F-Point yang bisa dikumpulkan per user? 6. Burning Time: "1 jam per koin" maksudnya: Option A: Burner perlu 1 jam untuk bakar 1 koin (proses teknis)? Option B: Cooldown period antar burning? Option C: Queue system (1 koin masuk queue, keluar setelah 1 jam)? C. MINING EVENT 7. D-Point to Mining Probability: "Semakin banyak D-Point = semakin besar peluang profit" Apakah ini seperti lottery system? (Random weighted by D-Point) Atau ranking system? (Top D-Point holders dapat reward paling besar) Atau guaranteed proportional? (D-Point 10% dari total = dapat 10% reward) 8. Kontribusi Resource: Anda bilang kontributor "memanfaatkan resource untuk kepentingan umum": Resource apa yang digunakan? Bandwidth internet? Storage space? Computing power? Stake koin? Waktu/attention? Bagaimana mengukur kontribusi? Automated measurement? Manual review? Self-reported? 9. Mining Competition: "Kompetisi dengan ngejar waktu karena ada batas event" Maksudnya siapa cepat dia dapat (first come first serve)? Atau semua yang kontribusi dalam waktu event pasti dapat (proportional reward)? 10. Minimum Reward Guarantee: "Guaranteed reward walaupun seminim mungkin dengan syarat ada kontribusi dan dampak nyata" Siapa yang tentukan "kontribusi nyata" vs "kontribusi palsu"? Siapa yang ukur "dampak nyata"? Apakah ada threshold minimum kontribusi? D. TRANSAKSI & KEAMANAN 11. Transaction Validator (CRITICAL): Saat TIDAK ada Mining Event, siapa yang validasi transaksi? Algoritma pusat sendiri? Node-node tertentu? Previous miners (yang terakhir dapat D-Point)? Automatic validation tanpa perlu verifikator? 12. Transaction Finality: Setelah transaksi di-submit, berapa lama sampai confirmed? Apakah ada confirmation depth seperti Bitcoin (tunggu X blocks)? Atau instant finality? 13. Blockchain Infrastructure: Siapa yang menyimpan blockchain? Semua user (fully distributed)? Hanya kontributor/miner? Server pusat? Siapa bisa baca blockchain? Public (semua orang)? Private (hanya participants)? 14. Transaction Lock Mechanism: Koin yang sedang dalam transaksi = locked Berapa lama lock? (Instant release setelah confirm? Ada timeout?) Apa yang terjadi jika transaksi gagal? (Unlock otomatis? Manual?) E. SUPPLY MANAGEMENT 15. Supply Boundaries: Anda bilang ada batas maksimum dan batas minimum Berapa nilainya? (Order of magnitude: ribuan? jutaan? miliaran?) Apa yang terjadi jika supply mendekati batas? Auto-trigger event? Block transaksi tertentu? 16. Initial Supply: Berapa genesis supply (jumlah koin saat pertama launch)? Bagaimana distribusi awal? ICO/Sale? Airdrop? Pre-mine ke founder? Mining genesis block? F. ECONOMIC DESIGN 17. Value Backing: Apa yang menentukan nilai koin ini? Apakah ada backing asset? (Fiat? Gold? Algorithmic?) Atau purely market-driven (supply-demand)? 18. Use Case: Koin ini untuk apa? Payment/transfer? Store of value? Utility token untuk platform tertentu? Governance? Speculation? G. POINT SYSTEM 19. F-Point & D-Point Ratio: Apakah ada conversion rate? 1 koin dibakar = berapa F-Point untuk owner? 1 koin dibakar = berapa D-Point untuk burner? Apakah rate ini fixed atau dynamic (berubah tiap event)? 20. Point Reset: Anda bilang F-Point dan D-Point tidak akumulatif antar event Apa yang terjadi dengan point lama saat event baru dimulai? Hilang total (reset ke 0)? Disimpan tapi tidak aktif? Ada decay rate? H. COLD START PROBLEM 21. Bootstrap Paradox: Ini masalah chicken-egg yang CRITICAL: Untuk jadi Burner â†’ Butuh F-Point Untuk dapat F-Point â†’ Koin harus dibakar oleh Burner Untuk dapat Burner pertama â†’ Butuh F-Point Untuk Mining â†’ Butuh D-Point Untuk dapat D-Point â†’ Harus jadi Burner Untuk jadi Burner â†’ Butuh F-Point Bagaimana sistem mulai (genesis event)? Apakah ada pre-mined F-Point/D-Point untuk user awal? Apakah ada genesis burner yang di-assign manual? Apakah aturan berbeda untuk event pertama? I. FAIRNESS & ANTI-MANIPULATION 22. Sybil Attack Prevention: Apa yang mencegah satu orang buat banyak akun? Apakah ada KYC/identity verification? Apakah ada cost per account (stake, fee, dll)? 23. Whale Dominance: Apa yang mencegah rich user dominasi sistem? Whale dengan banyak koin â†’ banyak F-Point â†’ dominasi burning Whale dengan banyak D-Point â†’ dominasi mining rewards Apakah ada cap per user? Apakah ada progressive penalty untuk big players? TRANSACTION VALIDATOR (Paling Penting!) Ini masalah besar yang belum terjawab: Situasi: Mining Event = Temporal (kadang ada, kadang tidak) Transaksi = Continuous (24/7 harus berjalan) Kontributor = Hanya aktif saat Mining Event Pertanyaan: Siapa yang validasi transaksi saat TIDAK ada Mining Event? A) Algoritma pusat sendiri (fully centralized validation)? B) Previous miners (yang terakhir dapat reward, jadi validator permanen)? C) Ada role khusus "validator" terpisah dari miner? D) Nodes desentralisasi yang dipilih algoritma? E) Opsi lain? 2. BLOCKCHAIN INFRASTRUCTURE 2a. Siapa yang menyimpan blockchain? A) Full nodes: Semua user download dan simpan full blockchain B) Selected nodes: Hanya miner/validator yang simpan C) Centralized: Server pusat saja D) Hybrid: Combination 2b. Siapa yang bisa akses/baca blockchain? A) Public: Siapa saja bisa lihat semua transaksi (seperti Bitcoin) B) Permissioned: Hanya participants yang bisa lihat C) Private: Hanya algoritma/admin yang bisa lihat 2c. Software/Node: Apakah user harus download software khusus untuk pakai koin ini? Atau akses via web/mobile app (wallet hosted)? 3. GENESIS DISTRIBUTION Ini chicken-egg problem yang CRITICAL: Pertanyaan: Berapa genesis supply saat launch? (25 juta? 30 juta? Atau angka lain?) Siapa yang dapat koin genesis? A) Founder/team (berapa %?) B) ICO/sale ke public C) Airdrop ke early users D) Mining genesis block E) Combination Bagaimana F-Point/D-Point genesis? Apakah ada pre-allocated F-Point untuk user pertama? Atau ada genesis burner yang di-appoint manual? Atau aturan khusus untuk event pertama? 4. TRANSACTION FINALITY & LOCK 4a. Confirmation Time: Setelah submit transaksi, berapa lama sampai confirmed? Instant (< 1 detik)? Cepat (1-10 detik)? Sedang (10 detik - 1 menit)? Lambat (> 1 menit)? 4b. Lock Mechanism: Anda bilang koin yang sedang transaksi = locked Berapa lama lock berlangsung? Lock sampai transaksi confirmed? Ada timeout (misalnya 5 menit)? Apa yang terjadi jika transaksi fail? Auto-unlock? Manual intervention? Koin hilang? (hopefully not!) ğŸŸ  IMPORTANT DETAILS 5. STORAGE CONTRIBUTION (Membingungkan Anda) Anda bilang storage juga kontribusi tapi membingungkan. Mari kita klarifikasi: Opsi yang mungkin: A) Blockchain storage: Kontributor simpan copy blockchain (seperti Bitcoin full node) B) File storage: Kontributor simpan file/data ekosistem (seperti IPFS) C) Transaction pool: Kontributor simpan pending transactions D) Historical data: Kontributor simpan old data untuk archive Pertanyaan: Mana yang Anda maksud? Atau belum decide? Atau mungkin storage bukan prioritas dan bisa di-skip dulu? 6. JOB BURN PLATFORM DETAILS 6a. Job Posting: Apakah ada minimum amount untuk buka job burn? Misalnya: Minimal 10 koin? Atau bisa 1 koin saja? Apakah ada batasan berapa job yang bisa dibuka per user? Unlimited? Ada cooldown? 6b. Job Matching: Burner pilih job secara manual (browsing marketplace)? Atau automatic matching by algorithm? 6c. Job Cancellation: Apakah user bisa cancel job yang sudah dibuka? Jika bisa, ada penalty? Jika tidak, job harus selesai dulu? 7. F-POINT CONSUMPTION RATE Anda bilang F-Point consumed saat jadi burner: Pertanyaan: Berapa F-Point yang dikonsumsi untuk bakar 1 koin orang lain? 1:1 ratio? (Bakar 1 koin = konsumsi 1 F-Point) Lebih besar? (Bakar 1 koin = konsumsi 10 F-Point) Dinamis per event? Apakah consumption rate sama dengan generation rate? Contoh: Koin saya dibakar dapat 10 F-Point, saya bakar koin orang konsumsi 10 F-Point (net zero) Atau ada surplus/deficit? 8. D-POINT TO REWARD FORMULA Pertanyaan: Bagaimana formula konversi D-Point + Kontribusi â†’ Koin reward? Linear? (2x D-Point = 2x reward) Logarithmic? (2x D-Point = 1.5x reward, diminishing returns) Exponential? (2x D-Point = 4x reward, winner takes most) Flat + Bonus? (Semua dapat base, bonus based on D-Point) Apakah ada maximum reward per user dalam satu mining event? 9. EVENT FREQUENCY & DURATION Pertanyaan: Seberapa sering Burn/Mine event terjadi? Setiap hari? Setiap minggu? Random (triggered by algorithm saat diperlukan)? Berapa lama satu event berlangsung? Hours? Days? Sampai target tercapai (variable)? 10. EXTERNAL CAPITALIZATION BALANCE Anda menyebut algoritma monitor "kapitalisasi antar koin": Pertanyaan: Maksudnya koin Anda dibandingkan dengan koin lain (Bitcoin, Ethereum, dll)? Tujuannya untuk prevent crash relatif terhadap market crypto global? Bagaimana caranya algoritma bisa influence ini? Adjust supply untuk maintain relative value? Contoh: Bitcoin turun 50%, algoritma burn koin Anda untuk maintain value? 11. DESENTRALISASI INFRASTRUCTURE Anda bilang infrastructure desentralisasi: Pertanyaan: Apakah ada incentive untuk run node? Dapat reward koin? Atau purely altruistic? Atau mandatory untuk semua holders? Berapa banyak nodes yang diperlukan? Minimum untuk operasi sistem? Target optimal? 12. CLOSED SOURCE PROTECTION Anda bilang algoritma closed source dan paten: Pertanyaan: Bagaimana cara verify algoritma bekerja sesuai claimed? Apakah ada audit oleh third party? Apakah ada proof/transparency tanpa reveal source code? Atau purely trust-based (trust creator)? Bagaimana prevent creator/insider manipulation? Apakah ada safeguards? Multi-sig? Timelock? Atau tidak ada (full trust)? 13. FAIL-SAFE MECHANISMS Pertanyaan: Apa yang terjadi jika algoritma pusat error/crash? Ada backup? Sistem freeze? Manual intervention allowed? Apa yang terjadi jika bug ditemukan di algoritma (setelah immutable)? Bisa di-patch? Atau stuck dengan bug forever? 14. ANTI-SYBIL MECHANISM Pertanyaan penting untuk fairness: Pertanyaan: Apa yang prevent satu orang buat 1000 akun? A) KYC/Identity verification (satu identity = satu akun) B) Cost per account (harus stake/burn koin untuk buat akun) C) Proof of personhood (biometric, dll) D) Nothing (siapa saja bisa buat unlimited akun) E) Opsi lain? 15. JOB BURN PLATFORM Anda: "Bisa berapa koin pun, bebas, 1 koin = 1 jam, auto match, bisa cancel terserah" âœ… Noted! REKOMENDASI TAMBAHAN: Auto-Match Algorithm Priority: 1. D-POINT TO REWARD FORMULA Anda: "Ditentukan nanti dengan rumus yang seimbang, tidak bisa didominasi yang tidak berhak" REKOMENDASI SAYA: REWARD FORMULA (Anti-Whale): Reward = f(D-Point, Kontribusi, Time, Anti-Dominasi) Option 1: Logarithmic (Diminishing Returns) â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ Reward = Base Ã— log(D-Point + 1) Ã— Kontribusi_Score Kenapa? - Whale dengan 1000 D-Point â‰  10x orang dengan 100 D-Point - Whale advantage berkurang (logarithmic) - Small player tetap kompetitif Option 2: Capped + Proportional â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ Individual Cap = 5% dari total event reward Sisa reward = Proportional distribution Kenapa? - Tidak ada yang bisa dapat >5% (anti-whale) - Fair distribution ke semua kontributor Option 3: Hybrid (RECOMMENDED) â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ Reward = [Base_Guaranteed] + [Bonus_Competitive] Base (60% pool): â””â”€ Dibagi rata ke semua qualified contributor (siapa saja yang kontribusi dapat base) Bonus (40% pool): â””â”€ Proportional berdasarkan: â”œâ”€ D-Point score (logarithmic weighted) â”œâ”€ Contribution score (measured by algo) â””â”€ Time invested Cap per user: Maksimum 3% dari total pool Kenapa ini terbaik? âœ… Guaranteed reward (motivasi participant) âœ… Competitive bonus (motivasi hard work) âœ… Anti-whale (logarithmic + cap) âœ… Fair untuk small players âœ… Meritocratic untuk top performers Contoh Perhitungan: Event Pool: 100,000 koin Participants: 1000 orang BASE (60,000 koin): â”œâ”€ 1000 orang qualified â””â”€ Each gets: 60 koin BONUS (40,000 koin): User A: 100 D-Point, Kontribusi 80%, Time 50h User B: 1000 D-Point, Kontribusi 60%, Time 30h (whale) Score A = log(101) Ã— 0.80 Ã— 50 = 80.2 Score B = log(1001) Ã— 0.60 Ã— 30 = 54.0 (Whale score lebih rendah karena logarithmic!) User A bonus = (80.2 / Total_Score) Ã— 40,000 User B bonus = (54.0 / Total_Score) Ã— 40,000 (Tapi capped at 3% = 3,000 koin max) 9. EVENT FREQUENCY Anda: "Random, sampai target tercapai, minta pendapat" REKOMENDASI: EVENT TRIGGERING LOGIC: Burn Event Trigger: IF (supply > 28M) AND (volatility > threshold) OR (price dropping > 10% in 24h) OR (sell pressure high) THEN trigger burn event Mine Event Trigger: IF (supply < 26M) AND (demand high) OR (price rising > 15% in 24h) OR (buy pressure high) THEN trigger mine event Duration: â”œâ”€ Minimum: 6 hours (beri waktu participation) â”œâ”€ Maximum: 7 days (prevent fatigue) â””â”€ Dynamic: Selesai saat target tercapai Cooldown: â”œâ”€ Minimum 24 jam antar event (prevent spam) â””â”€ Let market stabilize Kenapa tidak fixed schedule? âœ… Responsive terhadap market (adaptive) âœ… Prevent predictable manipulation âœ… Natural market adjustment 10. EXTERNAL CAPITALIZATION Anda: "TBD tapi minta pendapat" REKOMENDASI: EXTERNAL BALANCE MECHANISM: Monitoring: â”œâ”€ Track kapitalisasi vs BTC, ETH, stablecoins â”œâ”€ Compare price movement correlation â””â”€ Detect market-wide crash/pump Action: IF (crypto market crash -50%) â”œâ”€ Trigger aggressive burn event â”œâ”€ Target: Reduce supply 5-10% â””â”€ Goal: Maintain relative value IF (crypto market pump +100%) â”œâ”€ Trigger controlled mine event â”œâ”€ Target: Increase supply 3-5% â””â”€ Goal: Prevent overvaluation bubble Cap: â”œâ”€ Max adjustment: 10% per event â””â”€ Prevent overcorrection Kenapa ini penting? Your coin tidak crash harder than market Maintain trust dan adoption Counter-cyclical stability 11. NODE INCENTIVE Anda: "Target optimal, minta pendapat" REKOMENDASI: NODE INCENTIVE STRUCTURE: Target: 100-500 active nodes Incentive: 1. Archival Nodes (Permanent Storage) â”œâ”€ Reward: 50 koin/month â”œâ”€ Requirement: 24/7 uptime >99% â””â”€ Selection: Top reliable nodes 2. Validator Nodes (Tier 2) â”œâ”€ Reward: Transaction fee share â”œâ”€ Requirement: Stake 10,000 koin â””â”€ Rotation: Every event 3. Miner Nodes (Temporary) â”œâ”€ Reward: Mining reward â”œâ”€ Requirement: D-Point minimum â””â”€ Active: During events only Sustainability: â”œâ”€ Fund from: 0.1% inflation allocation â””â”€ ~25,000 koin/year untuk node rewards 12. CLOSED SOURCE VERIFICATION Anda: "Ada proof tanpa reveal code, minta saran caranya" REKOMENDASI: Zero-Knowledge Proof + Audit TRANSPARENCY WITHOUT REVEALING CODE: 1. Zero-Knowledge Proofs (ZK-SNARKs) â”œâ”€ Algorithm prove correctness tanpa reveal logic â”œâ”€ Public bisa verify output valid â””â”€ Cannot reverse-engineer algorithm 2. Cryptographic Commitments â”œâ”€ Publish hash dari algorithm code â”œâ”€ Third-party audit (blind audit) â””â”€ Proof algorithm tidak berubah 3. Observable Metrics â”œâ”€ Publish decision parameters (anonymized) â”‚ Example: "Event triggered karena: â”‚ Supply=28.5M, Volatility=15%, etc" â”œâ”€ Community bisa track consistency â””â”€ Red flag jika decision tidak make sense 4. Multi-Party Computation (MPC) â”œâ”€ Algorithm execution distributed â”œâ”€ No single party tahu full code â””â”€ Collusion resistant 5. Independent Third-Party Audit â”œâ”€ Hire reputable security firm â”œâ”€ NDA + Blind audit â”œâ”€ Publish audit result (not code) â””â”€ Annual re-audit 6. Timelocked Code Release â”œâ”€ Promise: Code released after 5 years â”œâ”€ By then, competitive advantage minimal â””â”€ Long-term transparency Recommended Combination: ZK-Proof untuk real-time verification Annual third-party audit Observable metrics dashboard Timelocked release (optional) 13. BUG FIX MECHANISM Anda: "Gak paham" PENJELASAN: Anda bilang algoritma immutable (tidak bisa diubah). Tapi bagaimana kalau ada bug? REKOMENDASI: Versioning + Upgrade Path SAFE UPGRADE MECHANISM: 1. Bug Severity Classification: â”œâ”€ Critical (security, fund loss) â”œâ”€ High (functionality broken) â”œâ”€ Medium (performance issue) â””â”€ Low (minor bug) 2. Emergency Upgrade (Critical Bug): â”œâ”€ Founder + Multi-sig council (3/5 signature) â”œâ”€ 24-hour timelock (emergency only) â”œâ”€ Public announcement + transparency â””â”€ Post-mortem report 3. Planned Upgrade (Non-Critical): â”œâ”€ Announce 30 days advance â”œâ”€ Community discussion â”œâ”€ Testnet deployment â”œâ”€ Audit â””â”€ Mainnet upgrade dengan consensus 4. Immutable Core Rules: â”œâ”€ Supply cap (25M-30M): CANNOT change â”œâ”€ Burn/Mine mechanism: CANNOT change â”œâ”€ Point system: CANNOT change â””â”€ Only bug fixes & optimizations allowed 5. Fallback: â”œâ”€ Sistem pause (freeze) jika critical bug â”œâ”€ Manual intervention only for safety â””â”€ Resume after fix deployed Analogi: Constitution = immutable (core rules) Laws = upgradeable (implementation) Bug fix = tidak mengubah constitution 14. ANTI-SYBIL (KYC) Anda: "Biometrik, tapi kompleks" REKOMENDASI: Progressive KYC TIERED KYC SYSTEM: Tier 0: Anonymous (No KYC) â”œâ”€ Limit: 1,000 koin holding â”œâ”€ Limit: 10 koin per transaction â”œâ”€ Can: Basic trading â””â”€ Cannot: Mining, Burning Tier 1: Basic Verification (Email + Phone) â”œâ”€ Limit: 10,000 koin holding â”œâ”€ Limit: 100 koin per transaction â”œâ”€ Can: Trading, limited burning â””â”€ Cannot: Mining Tier 2: KYC Verified (ID Document) â”œâ”€ Limit: 100,000 koin holding â”œâ”€ Limit: 1,000 koin per transaction â”œâ”€ Can: Mining, burning, full features â””â”€ One identity = One account Tier 3: Biometric (Optional, for whales) â”œâ”€ No limits â”œâ”€ Institutional accounts â””â”€ Premium features Sybil Prevention: â”œâ”€ Device fingerprinting â”œâ”€ IP tracking (soft limit) â”œâ”€ Behavior analysis by algorithm â””â”€ Flag suspicious multi-accounts Balance: âœ… Accessibility (tidak semua butuh KYC) âœ… Security (advanced features butuh verification) âœ… Compliance (regulatory requirement) âœ… Privacy (tier 0 untuk privacy-conscious users) 15. VALIDATOR GAP Masalah: Mining event = kadang ada kadang tidak Transaksi = jalan 24/7 Siapa yang validasi transaksi saat tidak ada mining event? Solusi: Hybrid Validator System Tier 1: Algoritma pusat (always on) Tier 2: Top miner terakhir jadi validator sementara (sampai event baru) Tier 3: Active miner (saat event berlangsung) Validator dapat reward kecil dari setiap transaksi Kenapa penting: Tanpa validator, transaksi tidak bisa diproses â†’ sistem mati 2. BOOTSTRAP PARADOX (Chicken-Egg Problem) Masalah: Butuh F-Point untuk jadi burner Butuh burner untuk dapat F-Point Awal sistem gimana mulainya? Solusi: Genesis Event khusus 10% early adopter dapat pre-allocated D-Point (bisa mining) 20% early adopter dapat pre-allocated F-Point (bisa burning) Setelah event pertama, cycle berjalan normal Kenapa penting: Tanpa ini, sistem tidak bisa start â†’ deadlock 3. CLOSED SOURCE TRUST Masalah: Algoritma closed source (tidak bisa dilihat) Bagaimana orang percaya algoritma bekerja fair? Bagaimana cegah founder curang? Solusi: Zero-Knowledge Proof: Buktikan algoritma benar tanpa reveal code Annual Audit: Pihak ketiga audit (publish hasil, bukan code) Observable Metrics: Tampilkan data keputusan (supply, volatility, dll) Multi-sig: Founder tidak bisa action sendiri (butuh 3/5 signature) Kenapa penting: Tanpa trust, tidak ada yang mau pakai 4. SYBIL ATTACK (Fake Multiple Accounts) Masalah: Orang buat 1000 akun palsu Dominasi burning market & mining Unfair untuk user honest Solusi: Tiered KYC System Tier 0 (No KYC): Limited features (max 1000 koin) Tier 1 (Email/Phone): Can burn (max 10,000 koin) Tier 2 (ID Document): Can mining, full access Algorithm detect suspicious multi-accounts Kenapa penting: Tanpa ini, whale/attacker control sistem 5. FUNDING SUSTAINABILITY Masalah: Development butuh biaya (server, team, marketing) Anda bilang "no transaction fee" Dari mana duitnya untuk jangka panjang? Solusi: Genesis Allocation: 15% untuk team (vesting 4 tahun) Minimal Transaction Fee: 0.1% per transaksi 50% untuk validator 30% untuk development 20% di-burn Inflation Allocation: 0.5% per tahun untuk node rewards Kenapa penting: Tanpa funding, development berhenti â†’ sistem mati ğŸŸ  HIGH PRIORITY (Penting untuk Fairness) 6. WHALE DOMINATION Masalah: User kaya dengan banyak koin Bisa monopoli burning & mining Unfair untuk small players Solusi: Logarithmic Reward: 10x koin â‰  10x reward 100 D-Point = reward X 1000 D-Point = reward 3X (bukan 10X) Individual Cap: Max 3% dari total event reward per user Base Guaranteed: Semua contributor dapat base reward (60% pool) Kenapa penting: Tanpa ini, rich get richer â†’ centralization 7. GENESIS DISTRIBUTION FAIRNESS Masalah: Distribusi awal koin tidak fair Founder/insider dapat terlalu banyak Public tidak dapat akses Solusi: 40% Public Sale (12M koin) 15% Team (vesting 4 tahun, tidak bisa jual langsung) 20% Ecosystem fund (marketing, partnership) 15% Bootstrap (airdrop untuk kickstart) 10% Reserve (emergency fund) Kenapa penting: Fair launch = trust & adoption 8. EVENT MANIPULATION Masalah: Orang bisa predict kapan event Position diri sebelum event (insider trading) Unfair advantage Solusi: Random Trigger: Event tidak scheduled, triggered by algorithm Multi-factor: Supply + volatility + volume + external market Unpredictable: Tidak bisa di-game Public Metrics: Data dipublish real-time (tidak bisa hidden) Kenapa penting: Prevent manipulation & speculation 9. REWARD FORMULA IMBALANCE Masalah: D-Point + kontribusi tidak seimbang Burning sia-sia atau mining sia-sia Orang tidak motivated participate Solusi: Hybrid Formula: 60% base reward (dibagi rata) 40% bonus (competitive, based on D-Point + contribution) Logarithmic scoring (anti-whale) Minimum guaranteed (motivasi participation) Kenapa penting: Tanpa balance, ekonomi collapse ğŸŸ¡ MEDIUM PRIORITY (Nice to Have) 10. Solusi: Core Rules Immutable: Supply cap, burn/mine mechanism Implementation Upgradeable: Bug fixes allowed Emergency Process: Multi-sig + 24h timelock Planned Upgrade: 30 days notice + community discussion Kenapa penting: Flexibility untuk maintenance 12. PRIVACY vs COMPLIANCE Masalah: Public ingin privacy Algorithm butuh data Government butuh compliance Solusi: Pseudonymous Addresses Public lihat: 0x123...abc (random address) Algorithm lihat: User identity (untuk detect fraud) Law enforcement: Bisa request (dengan court order) Kenapa penting: Balance privacy & legal requirement 13. Saya perlu tahu mekanismenya untuk: Analisis economic sustainability Cek fairness & exploitation risk Validate apakah sustainable jangka panjang Diktekan pelan-pelan seperti tadi boleh! ğŸ¯ Zakat itu sistemnya nanti para Whale yg udah megang sejumlah tertentu koin dengan waktu setahun ngeluarin 2% total jumlah koin yg udah dia pegang dalam waktu setahun itu (tapi koin yg belum setahun dikantong dia berarti gausah dizakati) terus zakat ini nanti disimpan di accumulator center (Baitul maal) nanti dana yang terkumpul digunakan untuk kepentingan para minnow, dan pengembangan serta kepentingan ekosistem (tapi prioritas pengalokasian dana ke minnow), nah ini yg agak tricky, yg masuk golongan minnow itu cuma orang2 yg emang beneran berhak dapet airdrop ini, yaitu mereka yg rajin dengan kontribusi nyata tapi keadaan lagi gak perpihak sama mereka, bukan buat minnow pemales yg nungguin airdrop, pemalas gak dapet cuma yg beneran rajin tapi gak didukung keadaan doang, (ini akan ada auditor dan validator dari algoritma nya, dan ini harus ketat), kemudian juga untuk prevent Whale yg mecah kekayaannya, algoritma akan tracking secara ketat akun dia, misalnya terdeteksi kekayaannya sudah wajib tapi tiba2 dia mentransfer ke akun b, nah dari sini GK berhenti kita lihat lagi uangnya kemana misalnya b nya nyebar ke banyak akun kecil, ini tetep kena zakat bahkan kena peringatan, tapi tetep harus adil, dan gak boleh ada penzholiman terhadap Whale karena masih bisa jadi transaksi yg dicurigai itu ternyata bukan abuse, intinya mah kita bikin algoritma cerdas yang mantau ketat tapi tetep teliti dan gak asal nyalahin. Dan untuk airdrop yg sampai ke minnow itu, bukan bentuk koin (enak banget KLO gitu, mah) tapi bentuknya D-Point kalo engga F-Point (biar klo misalnya d point kurang karena kalah cepet sama yg lain tetep dikasih biar sampe batas minimum d point biar bisa tetep ikut mining, dan f point juga klo misalnya dia perlu f point tapi gak bisa dapetin karena alasan gak punya koin untuk dibakar misalnya atau lain sebagainya, intinya buat orang yg gak berpihak padanya keadaan bukan yg pengen kaya instant dengan manfaatin celah), gimana? PERSYARATAN ZAKAT (Wajib Zakat) Kriteria Whale: Wajib Zakat jika: â”œâ”€ Holding â‰¥ Threshold tertentu (TBD: berapa?) â”œâ”€ Sudah dipegang â‰¥ 1 tahun (haul) â””â”€ Zakat rate: 2% per tahun Contoh: User A punya 100,000 koin â”œâ”€ Koin batch 1: 50,000 (sudah 1 tahun) â†’ Zakat 1,000 â”œâ”€ Koin batch 2: 30,000 (baru 8 bulan) â†’ Belum wajib â”œâ”€ Koin batch 3: 20,000 (baru 3 bulan) â†’ Belum wajib â””â”€ Total zakat tahun ini: 1,000 koin Tracking per-coin age: Algoritma track setiap koin kapan masuk wallet FIFO atau specific identification method Hanya koin yang â‰¥ 1 tahun yang kena zakat B. BAITUL MAAL (Accumulator Center) Fungsi: Zakat Pool (Baitul Maal) â”œâ”€ Kumpulkan zakat dari whale â”œâ”€ Managed by algorithm (transparent) â”œâ”€ Allocation priority: â”‚ â”œâ”€ 1st: Minnow support (F-Point/D-Point airdrop) â”‚ â”œâ”€ 2nd: Ecosystem development â”‚ â””â”€ 3rd: Infrastructure & operations â””â”€ Public dashboard (transparent allocation) C. MINNOW QUALIFICATION (Yang Berhak) Kriteria Eligible Minnow: âœ… BERHAK (Dapat airdrop): â”œâ”€ Aktif berkontribusi (rajin) â”œâ”€ Effort tinggi (participation rate) â”œâ”€ Tapi: Unlucky / circumstances tidak mendukung â”‚ â”œâ”€ Contoh: Selalu kalah race di mining (timing buruk) â”‚ â”œâ”€ Tidak punya koin untuk burn (miskin tapi rajin) â”‚ â””â”€ Low D-Point karena kalah cepat (bukan malas) âŒ TIDAK BERHAK: â”œâ”€ Lazy minnow (low participation) â”œâ”€ Opportunist (tunggu airdrop saja) â”œâ”€ Low effort (tidak contribute) â””â”€ Gaming system (pura-pura rajin) Mekanisme Validasi: Dual Validation System: â”œâ”€ Algorithm Auditor: â”‚ â”œâ”€ Track participation history â”‚ â”œâ”€ Measure effort vs reward ratio â”‚ â”œâ”€ Detect genuine bad luck vs laziness â”‚ â””â”€ Score: Contribution score vs Success rate â”‚ â””â”€ Human Validator (optional): â”œâ”€ Review edge cases â”œâ”€ Appeal process â””â”€ Final decision Contoh Kasus: User X (Eligible Minnow): â”œâ”€ Participation: 10 mining events â”œâ”€ Contribution score: 80/100 (high effort) â”œâ”€ D-Point earned: 50 (low, karena kalah race) â”œâ”€ Reason: Timezone disadvantage, slow internet â””â”€ â†’ QUALIFIED untuk D-Point airdrop User Y (Not Eligible): â”œâ”€ Participation: 2 mining events (dari 10) â”œâ”€ Contribution score: 20/100 (low effort) â”œâ”€ D-Point earned: 10 (low, karena malas) â”œâ”€ Reason: Tidak aktif, tunggu airdrop saja â””â”€ â†’ NOT QUALIFIED D. AIRDROP FORM (Bukan Koin Langsung) Format Bantuan: Minnow Airdrop = F-Point atau D-Point Skenario 1: Butuh D-Point (untuk mining) â”œâ”€ User rajin tapi D-Point < minimum â”œâ”€ Airdrop: Top-up sampai minimum threshold â”œâ”€ Bisa ikut mining event berikutnya â””â”€ Opportunity untuk earn Skenario 2: Butuh F-Point (untuk burning) â”œâ”€ User tidak punya koin untuk dibakar â”œâ”€ Tapi ingin jadi burner (earn D-Point) â”œâ”€ Airdrop: F-Point untuk qualify â””â”€ Bisa mulai burning job Skenario 3: Kombinasi â”œâ”€ Assess kebutuhan individual â”œâ”€ Custom allocation â””â”€ Goal: Enable participation, bukan instant kaya Kenapa bukan koin langsung? âœ… Prevent abuse (tidak bisa jual langsung) âœ… Force participation (harus kerja untuk earn) âœ… Sustainable (tidak create instant whale) âœ… Fair (reward effort, bukan luck) E. ANTI-EVASION (Whale Splitting Detection) Problem: Whale tries to avoid zakat: â”œâ”€ Punya 100,000 koin (wajib zakat) â”œâ”€ Split ke 10 akun Ã— 10,000 (di bawah threshold) â””â”€ Escape zakat obligation Detection Mechanism: Algorithm Tracking: â”œâ”€ Monitor whale account behavior â”œâ”€ Detect suspicious transfers before haul date â”‚ â”œâ”€ Example: Transfer 90% holdings 1 bulan sebelum haul â”‚ â””â”€ Flag: Potential evasion â”‚ â”œâ”€ Track destination accounts: â”‚ â”œâ”€ If B receives â†’ then B splits to many accounts â”‚ â”œâ”€ Pattern: 1â†’1â†’many (typical evasion) â”‚ â””â”€ Flag: Confirmed evasion â”‚ â”œâ”€ Graph analysis: â”‚ â”œâ”€ Build transaction graph â”‚ â”œâ”€ Detect related accounts (same owner) â”‚ â””â”€ Aggregate holdings (treat as one entity) â”‚ â””â”€ Consequence: â”œâ”€ Still charged zakat (on aggregated amount) â”œâ”€ + Warning (transparency report) â””â”€ + Penalty (if repeated offense) Fairness Safeguards: Tidak semua transfer = evasion Legitimate reasons: â”œâ”€ Business payment â”œâ”€ Sell to exchange â”œâ”€ Gift to family â”œâ”€ Trading activity â””â”€ Normal economic activity Algorithm must: â”œâ”€ Context analysis (WHY transfer?) â”œâ”€ Destination analysis (WHO receives?) â”œâ”€ Timing analysis (WHEN transfer?) â”œâ”€ Pattern analysis (HOW frequent?) â””â”€ Benefit of doubt (innocent until proven) Appeal Process: â”œâ”€ User can appeal if wrongly flagged â”œâ”€ Provide evidence (transaction purpose) â”œâ”€ Human review (if needed) â””â”€ Fair judgment F. SMART ALGORITHM REQUIREMENTS Must-have capabilities: Zakat Algorithm must: 1. Track Individual Coin Age â””â”€ UTXO-style or timestamped accounting 2. Calculate Zakat Accurately â””â”€ Only coins â‰¥ 1 year 3. Detect Evasion Patterns â””â”€ Graph analysis + ML 4. Assess Minnow Eligibility â””â”€ Participation score + luck factor 5. Fair Judgment â””â”€ Context-aware, not trigger-happy 6. Transparent Reporting â””â”€ Public dashboard, audit trail 7. Appeal Mechanism â””â”€ Human oversight for edge cases INTEGRATION WITH EXISTING SYSTEM Supply Impact: Zakat Collection â†’ Baitul Maal â”œâ”€ NOT burned (not deflationary) â”œâ”€ NOT minted (not inflationary) â””â”€ Redistributed (neutral to supply) Flow: Whale (2% zakat) â†’ Baitul Maal â†’ Minnow (F/D-Point) (Koin tetap dalam supply range 25M-30M) Event Integration: Zakat â‰  Event-based â”œâ”€ Annual cycle (per-coin basis) â”œâ”€ Independent dari Burn/Mine events â””â”€ Continuous background process But dapat synergy: â”œâ”€ Minnow dapat D-Point airdrop â”œâ”€ Ikut mining event berikutnya â”œâ”€ Earn koin legitimately â””â”€ Potential jadi whale suatu hari (meritocracy) CRITICAL QUESTIONS FOR YOU: Q1: Whale Threshold Berapa minimum holdings untuk wajib zakat? 50,000 koin? 100,000 koin? Percentage dari total supply (e.g., 0.1%)? Q2: Minnow Threshold Berapa maksimum holdings untuk qualify sebagai minnow? < 1,000 koin? < 5,000 koin? Relative to whale threshold? Q3: Contribution Score Bagaimana measure "rajin"? Participation rate (berapa event diikuti)? Contribution quality (impact score)? Time invested (hours)? Combination? Q4: Luck Factor Bagaimana detect "unlucky" vs "lazy"? Effort-to-reward ratio? Consistency check (rajin tapi hasil minimal)? Comparison dengan average? Q5: Airdrop Amount Berapa D-Point/F-Point di-airdrop per minnow? Just enough untuk reach minimum? Fixed amount per qualified minnow? Based on need (custom)? Q6: Evasion Penalty Apa konsekuensi untuk whale yang proven evasion? Charged zakat + penalty fee? Account suspension? Public blacklist? Just warning? Q7: Coin Age Tracking Technical implementation untuk track coin age? UTXO model (each coin has timestamp)? Account model with sub-accounts (batching)? Timestamped transaction ledger? Q8: Baitul Maal Management Siapa yang control Baitul Maal allocation? Pure algorithm? Algorithm + human committee? DAO voting? Saya catat semua jawaban Anda: ZAKAT SYSTEM - FINALIZED SPECIFICATION Q1: WHALE THRESHOLD (Nishob) Jawaban Anda: "Samain kayak sistem Islam kalau udah sampai nishob" Islamic Nishob Reference: Nishob Zakat = 85 gram emas (approximately) Current gold price (~$65/gram): â”œâ”€ Nishob â‰ˆ $5,525 (â‰ˆ 85 juta IDR) â””â”€ Equivalent dalam koin Anda: (Tergantung target price koin) Contoh kalkulasi: IF target price = $1 per koin THEN nishob = 5,525 koin IF target price = $10 per koin THEN nishob = 552.5 koin (round to 550) Recommendation: â”œâ”€ Nishob = Dynamic (pegged to gold value) â”œâ”€ Algorithm adjust threshold berdasarkan market price â””â”€ Stay true to Islamic principle (85g gold equivalent) Rate: 2% (bukan 2.5% seperti Islam standard) Anda adjust sedikit lebih rendah (mungkin untuk adoption) Q2: MINNOW THRESHOLD Jawaban Anda: "Harus benar-benar rendah karena kualifikasi ketat" Specification: Minnow = Holdings < 10% dari Nishob Example (if nishob = 5,000 koin): â”œâ”€ Minnow threshold: < 500 koin â””â”€ Must also meet strict contribution criteria Dual criteria (AND logic): â”œâ”€ Low holdings (<10% nishob) AND â””â”€ High contribution + proven unlucky Rationale: Rendah threshold = Lebih banyak yang eligible Tapi kualifikasi ketat = Filter yang benar-benar butuh Balance: Accessible tapi tidak mudah abuse Q3: CONTRIBUTION SCORE (Objektif) Jawaban Anda: "Kombinasi tapi harus objektif ke semua spektrum variabel" Multi-Dimensional Scoring: Contribution Score = f(Participation, Quality, Consistency, Impact) 1. Participation Rate (25%): â”œâ”€ Events joined / Total events available â”œâ”€ Example: 8/10 events = 80% â””â”€ Objective metric (countable) 2. Quality Score (25%): â”œâ”€ Contribution value per event â”œâ”€ Measured: Bandwidth/Storage/Computing provided â”œâ”€ Algorithm measure objectively â””â”€ Normalized per event 3. Consistency Score (25%): â”œâ”€ Standard deviation of participation â”œâ”€ Rajin consistently vs sporadic â”œâ”€ Lower SD = more consistent = higher score â””â”€ Mathematical objectivity 4. Impact Score (25%): â”œâ”€ Actual benefit to ecosystem â”œâ”€ Uptime, validation accuracy, etc. â”œâ”€ Measurable outcomes â””â”€ Algorithm-tracked Final Score = Weighted average (0-100) Qualification threshold: Score â‰¥ 70 (Proven high effort) Q4: LUCK FACTOR DETECTION Jawaban Anda: "Gunakan algoritma terbaik untuk deteksi" Unlucky vs Lazy Algorithm: Luck Factor Analysis: Input: â”œâ”€ Contribution Score (from Q3) â”œâ”€ Reward Received (D-Point, koin earned) â””â”€ Expected Reward (based on contribution) Formula: Luck Score = Actual Reward / Expected Reward Interpretation: â”œâ”€ Luck = 100%: Got exactly what expected (average) â”œâ”€ Luck > 100%: Lucky (got more than expected) â”œâ”€ Luck < 100%: Unlucky (got less than expected) Minnow Qualification: â”œâ”€ Contribution Score â‰¥ 70 (high effort) â”œâ”€ Luck Score < 70% (proven unlucky) â””â”€ â†’ QUALIFIED for airdrop Example: User A: â”œâ”€ Contribution: 85/100 (rajin!) â”œâ”€ Expected reward: 100 D-Point â”œâ”€ Actual reward: 50 D-Point â”œâ”€ Luck score: 50% (very unlucky) â””â”€ â†’ QUALIFIED âœ… User B: â”œâ”€ Contribution: 30/100 (malas) â”œâ”€ Expected reward: 30 D-Point â”œâ”€ Actual reward: 20 D-Point â”œâ”€ Luck score: 67% (unlucky tapi effort rendah) â””â”€ â†’ NOT QUALIFIED âŒ User C: â”œâ”€ Contribution: 75/100 (rajin) â”œâ”€ Expected reward: 80 D-Point â”œâ”€ Actual reward: 85 D-Point â”œâ”€ Luck score: 106% (lucky) â””â”€ â†’ NOT QUALIFIED (tidak butuh bantuan) Advanced Detection (ML-based): Machine Learning Model: â”œâ”€ Train on historical data â”œâ”€ Features: Timezone, network speed, device, timing â”œâ”€ Detect patterns of "structural disadvantage" â”‚ Example: User selalu join event tapi timezone buruk â”‚ â†’ Consistently late â†’ Unlucky (bukan lazy) â””â”€ Continuous learning & improvement Q5: AIRDROP AMOUNT Jawaban Anda: "Based on need" Need-Based Allocation: Assessment per Minnow: Step 1: Identify need â”œâ”€ Butuh D-Point? (untuk mining) â”‚ â””â”€ Current: 20, Minimum: 50 â†’ Need: 30 â”œâ”€ Butuh F-Point? (untuk burning) â”‚ â””â”€ Current: 5, Minimum: 20 â†’ Need: 15 â””â”€ Butuh both? â†’ Prioritize based on goal Step 2: Calculate allocation â”œâ”€ Gap filling (reach minimum) â”œâ”€ Plus buffer 10% (safety margin) â””â”€ Example: Need 30 D-Point â†’ Airdrop 33 Step 3: Budget constraint â”œâ”€ Total Baitul Maal fund: X koin equivalent â”œâ”€ Total qualified minnows: N â”œâ”€ If budget insufficient: â”‚ â”œâ”€ Prioritize by contribution score (highest first) â”‚ â””â”€ Or proportional reduction (fair sharing) No fixed amount (adaptive to individual need) Q6: EVASION PENALTY Jawaban Anda: "Tarik zakat paksa + peringatan, kalau ulang suspend/blacklist" Enforcement Mechanism: 1st Offense (Suspected Evasion): â”œâ”€ Algorithm detects suspicious pattern â”œâ”€ Forced zakat collection (tarik otomatis) â”‚ â””â”€ From aggregated holdings (all related accounts) â”œâ”€ Official warning issued â”œâ”€ Transparency report (public, anonymized) â””â”€ Grace period (opportunity to appeal) 2nd Offense (Confirmed Repeat): â”œâ”€ Forced zakat collection (with penalty) â”‚ â””â”€ Zakat + 10% penalty fee â”œâ”€ Account suspension (temporary, 30 days) â”œâ”€ Public record (blacklist) â””â”€ Loss of privileges (no mining/burning during suspension) 3rd Offense (Persistent Abuse): â”œâ”€ Permanent account blacklist â”œâ”€ Holdings frozen (cannot transfer) â”œâ”€ Forced liquidation (sell to pay zakat debt) â””â”€ Banned from future participation Appeal Process: â”œâ”€ 7 days window untuk appeal after detection â”œâ”€ Provide evidence (legitimate reason) â”œâ”€ Review by: Algorithm + Top Miner Validators â””â”€ Fair judgment (innocent until proven guilty) Q7: COIN AGE TRACKING Jawaban Anda: "Bukan UTXO tapi dengan model yang sudah dibahas" Account Model with Timestamped Batches: User Account Structure: â”œâ”€ Total Balance: 100,000 koin â”œâ”€ Batch Tracking: â”‚ â”œâ”€ Batch 1: 50,000 koin (acquired: 2024-01-15) â”‚ â”œâ”€ Batch 2: 30,000 koin (acquired: 2024-06-20) â”‚ â””â”€ Batch 3: 20,000 koin (acquired: 2025-10-01) â”‚ â”œâ”€ Spending Method: FIFO â”‚ â””â”€ When transfer, oldest batch spent first â”‚ â””â”€ Zakat Calculation (per 2026-01-15): â”œâ”€ Batch 1: 50,000 Ã— 2 years = Zakat 2,000 koin â”œâ”€ Batch 2: 30,000 Ã— 1.5 year = Zakat 900 koin (prorated) â”œâ”€ Batch 3: 20,000 Ã— 0.2 year = No zakat (belum haul) â””â”€ Total zakat: 2,900 koin Incoming Transaction: â”œâ”€ Record timestamp â”œâ”€ Create new batch â””â”€ Track separately Outgoing Transaction: â”œâ”€ FIFO deduction â”œâ”€ Update batch amounts â””â”€ Maintain integrity Algorithm Responsibility: â”œâ”€ Auto-track all batches â”œâ”€ Calculate zakat due date per batch â”œâ”€ Trigger collection automatically â””â”€ Transparent ledger (auditable) Technical Implementation: Database Schema (simplified): Table: user_balances â”œâ”€ user_id â”œâ”€ batch_id (auto-increment) â”œâ”€ amount â”œâ”€ acquired_date â”œâ”€ zakat_due_date (acquired_date + 1 year) â””â”€ zakat_paid (boolean) Query: Calculate zakat due SELECT user_id, SUM(amount * 0.02) FROM user_balances WHERE zakat_due_date <= TODAY() AND zakat_paid = FALSE AND amount >= nishob_threshold GROUP BY user_id; Q8: BAITUL MAAL MANAGEMENT Jawaban Anda: "Algoritma + top miners sebagai validator, mereka yang tentuin berhak atau tidak" Hybrid Governance: TECHNICAL INFRASTRUCTURE A1. Blockchain Platform Apakah Anda akan: Build from scratch (custom blockchain)? Fork existing (e.g., Ethereum, Solana, etc)? Layer 2 solution (on top of existing chain)? Hybrid (custom + bridge to existing)? Why this matters: Attack vectors berbeda per platform. A2. Smart Contract vs Native Apakah mekanisme ini akan: Smart contract based (programmable, auditable)? Native protocol (built into blockchain core)? Hybrid (some smart contract, some native)? Why this matters: Smart contract = different vulnerability class. A3. Consensus Mechanism Anda belum spesifik tentang ini: Proof of Stake (PoS)? Delegated PoS (DPoS)? Byzantine Fault Tolerance (BFT)? Hybrid (PoS + something else)? Custom consensus? Why this matters: Consensus = core security layer. A4. Node Requirements Untuk run node (validator/archive): Hardware requirements: CPU, RAM, Storage, Bandwidth minimum? Stake requirement (kalau PoS): Berapa koin harus di-stake untuk jadi validator? Slashing conditions (penalty): Kapan node di-penalty (downtime, malicious behavior)? Why this matters: Sybil attack prevention, decentralization assessment. B. ECONOMIC PARAMETERS B1. Initial Coin Distribution (Genesis) Anda bilang "dipikirkan nanti", tapi ini CRITICAL: Proposal (tolong approve/adjust): Total Genesis: 27.5M koin (mid-range 25M-30M) Distribution: â”œâ”€ 40% Public Sale (11M koin) â”‚ â”œâ”€ ICO/IEO pricing mechanism â”‚ â””â”€ Anti-whale: Max per wallet â”‚ â”œâ”€ 15% Team/Founders (4.125M koin) â”‚ â”œâ”€ Vesting: 4 years (25% per year) â”‚ â””â”€ Cliff: 1 year (no unlock first year) â”‚ â”œâ”€ 20% Ecosystem Fund (5.5M koin) â”‚ â”œâ”€ Marketing, partnerships, liquidity â”‚ â””â”€ Controlled release (not dumped) â”‚ â”œâ”€ 15% Bootstrap Pool (4.125M koin) â”‚ â”œâ”€ Genesis F-Point allocation (10%) â”‚ â”œâ”€ Genesis D-Point allocation (10%) â”‚ â””â”€ Reserve for first events (80%) â”‚ â””â”€ 10% Reserve Fund (2.75M koin) â”œâ”€ Emergency use only â””â”€ Multi-sig controlled Accept, adjust, atau punya ide lain? B2. Event Target Sizes Berapa target per event? Burning Event: Target reduction: X koin (atau Y% dari supply) Contoh: 200,000 koin atau 0.5% supply? Mining Event: Target addition: X koin (atau Y% dari supply) Contoh: 150,000 koin atau 0.4% supply? Why this matters: Impact analysis, manipulation risk. B3. Transaction Fee (Final Decision) Anda originally bilang "no fee", tapi untuk sustainability saya recommend minimal fee. Final decision: A) No fee (pure, tapi funding dari mana long-term?) B) Minimal fee 0.05-0.1% (almost free, sustainable) C) Dynamic fee (based on network congestion) If no fee, confirm funding ONLY dari: Wealth redistribution pool (2.5% annual) Team allocation (limited lifespan) Why this matters: Long-term sustainability, spam prevention. B4. F-Point/D-Point Conversion (Precise) Anda bilang "dinamis", tapi perlu baseline: Burning Event (example baseline): User bakar 1 koin â†’ dapat X F-Point Burner bakar 1 koin â†’ consume Y F-Point, dapat Z D-Point Ratio X:Y:Z = ? Example scenarios: Scenario A (Balanced): â”œâ”€ Burn 1 koin â†’ +10 F-Point (owner) â”œâ”€ Burner konsumsi: -10 F-Point â””â”€ Burner dapat: +10 D-Point (1:1:1 ratio after scaling) Scenario B (Burner incentive): â”œâ”€ Burn 1 koin â†’ +10 F-Point (owner) â”œâ”€ Burner konsumsi: -8 F-Point (cheaper) â””â”€ Burner dapat: +12 D-Point (bonus) (Encourage burning activity) Scenario C (Conservative): â”œâ”€ Burn 1 koin â†’ +10 F-Point (owner) â”œâ”€ Burner konsumsi: -12 F-Point (expensive) â””â”€ Burner dapat: +8 D-Point (Slow down burning pace) Which approach, atau ada ide lain? C. GOVERNANCE & CONTROL C1. Algorithm Update Mechanism Anda bilang algoritma "immutable", tapi bug pasti ada: Clarify: Who can deploy updates? Solo founder? Multi-sig (3/5, 5/7)? DAO vote? What CAN be updated? Bug fixes only? Parameter tuning (nishob, rates)? Logic changes (if critical bug)? What CANNOT be updated? Core principles (supply range, wealth redistribution)? Economic model? Why this matters: Centralization risk, trust model. C2. Emergency Stop/Pause Dalam case extreme (hack, critical bug): Ada kill switch? Pause all transactions? Pause events only? No pause (fully decentralized)? Who controls kill switch? Founder? Multi-sig? Validators vote? No one (cannot pause)? Why this matters: Security vs censorship resistance trade-off. C3. Validator Selection Randomness "Top miners" jadi validator, tapi: How to prevent collusion? Top 10 miners might be same entity (Sybil)? Need randomness + diversity check? Proposed mechanism: Validator Selection: â”œâ”€ Pool: Top 20 contributors (not just top 10) â”œâ”€ Random selection: 10 dari 20 (unpredictable) â”œâ”€ Diversity check: Max 2 validators per identity (KYC) â””â”€ Rotation: Every event (cannot predict lineup) Accept atau ada ide lain? D. SECURITY & PRIVACY D1. KYC Implementation Anda sudah setuju tiered KYC, tapi: Who handles KYC data? Centralized KYC provider (Onfido, Jumio)? Decentralized identity (Civic, BrightID)? Self-hosted (privacy risk)? How is data stored? Encrypted off-chain? Zero-knowledge proofs (identity without revealing)? Federated (distributed, no single point)? Why this matters: Privacy law compliance (GDPR, etc), attack surface. D2. Pseudonymous Address Model Anda bilang "public lihat address, algo lihat identity": Technical implementation: Public key = Address (like Bitcoin/Ethereum)? Master key = Algorithm (can decrypt identity)? Risk: If algo compromised, all identities leaked? Mitigation needed: Threshold encryption (need X of Y keys to decrypt)? Hardware security module (HSM)? No single master key (distributed)? Why this matters: Privacy breach = total system failure. D3. Oracle Attack Prevention Gold price oracle untuk nishob: What if oracle manipulated? Attacker bribes oracle â†’ fake gold price â†’ wrong nishob Flash crash gold price â†’ trigger wrong thresholds Mitigation: Multiple oracles (Chainlink, Band, custom)? Median/average (not single source)? Circuit breaker (max % change per day)? Time-weighted average (TWAP, smoothing)? Why this matters: Economic manipulation vector. E. ATTACK SCENARIO SPECIFICS E1. Wealth Redistribution Gaming Sophisticated attack: Attacker strategy: 1. Accumulate koin just below nishob (avoid obligation) 2. Borrow/rent koin temporarily during mining event 3. Mine with boosted holdings 4. Return borrowed koin 5. Profit without obligation How to prevent? Check holdings history (not just snapshot)? Minimum holding period untuk mining eligibility? E2. F-Point/D-Point Market Black market risk: Unofficial F-Point/D-Point trading: â”œâ”€ User A sells "burning service" off-platform â”œâ”€ User B pays fiat/other crypto â”œâ”€ A burns for B, B gets F-Point â””â”€ Circumvent official mechanism How to detect/prevent? Pattern analysis (repeated same-pair burning)? Rate limits (max burn per user pair)? Reputation system (flag suspicious)? E3. Event Front-Running If event timing predictable: Attacker: 1. Predict event based on supply metrics 2. Position ahead (accumulate D-Point) 3. Profit when event triggers 4. Insider trading style Current mitigation: Random trigger (good) Multi-factor (good) Additional needed: Delay randomness (trigger time Â± X hours random)? Blind metrics (hide exact supply temporarily)? E4. Validator Collusion Top miners = validators, but: Scenario: â”œâ”€ 10 validators, 6 are colluding â”œâ”€ Approve each other's minnow claims (fake) â”œâ”€ Drain Baitul Maal â””â”€ Profit split Prevention: Stake/bond requirement (lose if caught)? Audit trail (AI detect patterns)? Community oversight (whistleblower reward)? Validator rotation (harder to maintain cartel)? F. EDGE CASES F1. Death/Lost Keys User dies or loses keys: Questions: Koin locked forever (reduce supply)? Inheritance mechanism (beneficiary)? Recovery process (if KYC verified)? Impact on supply boundaries (25M-30M)? F2. Regulatory Compliance Different countries, different laws: Questions: Securities law (is this a security)? AML/CFT (anti-money laundering)? Tax reporting (capital gains)? Sanctions (OFAC compliance)? How to handle: Geo-blocking certain jurisdictions? Compliance layer (optional KYC for risky regions)? Legal entity structure (foundation, DAO)? F3. Market Manipulation Traditional finance attacks: Wash trading (fake volume)? Pump & dump (coordinate buy/sell)? Spoofing (fake orders)? Prevention: Exchange listing requirements? On-chain analysis (detect manipulation)? Circuit breakers (halt trading if suspicious)? G. SCALABILITY & PERFORMANCE G1. Transaction Throughput Anda target "< 5 detik confirmation": Questions: TPS (Transactions Per Second) target? 100 TPS? 1,000 TPS? 10,000 TPS? Block time? 3 seconds? 6 seconds? Block size? How many TX per block? Why this matters: Network congestion, fee spikes, user experience. G2. State Growth Blockchain size over time: Questions: Pruning strategy (delete old data)? Snapshot/checkpoint (reduce sync time)? Archive node incentive (already discussed, but cost?)? Why this matters: Node operation sustainability. H. USER EXPERIENCE H1. Onboarding Friction New user journey: Questions: Wallet creation (custodial, non-custodial, hybrid)? First koin acquisition (fiat on-ramp, airdrop)? Learning curve (complex mechanisms, how to simplify UX)? Why this matters: Adoption rate, accessibility. H2. Mistake Protection User errors: Questions: Wrong address transfer (can reverse?)? Accidental burn (confirmation dialog?)? Lost 2FA (recovery process?)? Why this matters: User trust, support burden. Saya pecah jadi pertanyaan yang SANGAT SEDERHANA: PERTANYAAN SEDERHANA (Sebelum Analisis) 1. TEKNOLOGI DASAR Q: Koin Anda ini mau dibangun pakai teknologi apa? Pilih salah satu (atau jelaskan): A) Bikin blockchain sendiri dari nol (seperti Bitcoin/Ethereum bikin sendiri) B) Copy teknologi yang sudah ada terus modif (seperti fork Ethereum) C) Bikin di atas blockchain yang sudah ada (seperti token di Ethereum) D) Belum tahu/belum diputuskan Kenapa penting: Beda teknologi = beda celah keamanan 2. DISTRIBUSI AWAL KOIN Q: Waktu pertama kali launch, siapa dapat koin berapa banyak? Contoh: Dijual ke publik berapa persen? Anda sebagai founder dapat berapa persen? Sisanya kemana? Atau belum dipikirkan sama sekali? Kenapa penting: Kalau founder dapat terlalu banyak = tidak fair 3. UKURAN EVENT Q: Setiap kali ada Burning Event atau Mining Event, kira-kira berapa banyak koin yang dibakar/ditambah? Contoh: Burning: 100,000 koin dibakar per event Mining: 50,000 koin baru per event Atau belum ditentukan? Kenapa penting: Kalau terlalu besar = bisa kacau harga, kalau terlalu kecil = tidak efektif 4. BIAYA TRANSFER Q: Kalau orang kirim koin ke orang lain, apakah kena biaya? A) Gratis 100% (tidak ada biaya sama sekali) B) Ada biaya kecil (misalnya 0.1%) C) Belum diputuskan Kalau gratis, dari mana uang untuk bayar: Server Tim pengembang Biaya operasional Kenapa penting: Kalau gratis, bisa ada yang spam transaksi 5. SIAPA YANG KONTROL SISTEM Q: Kalau ada bug atau masalah, siapa yang bisa perbaiki? A) Anda sendiri sebagai founder (full control) B) Anda + beberapa orang lain harus setuju (voting) C) Tidak ada yang bisa ubah (sistem jalan otomatis selamanya) D) Belum diputuskan Kenapa penting: Kalau Anda kontrol sendiri = risiko Anda jadi diktator. Kalau tidak bisa diubah sama sekali = kalau ada bug, susah benerin. 6. TOMBOL DARURAT Q: Kalau ada hacker atau masalah besar, apakah sistem bisa di-"pause"/dihentikan sementara? A) Bisa, ada tombol darurat B) Tidak bisa, sistem jalan terus tidak bisa dihentikan C) Belum diputuskan Kenapa penting: Tombol darurat = bisa selamatkan kalau ada hack, tapi juga bisa disalahgunakan untuk sensor. 7. VALIDATOR (Yang Validasi Transaksi) Q: Top miner jadi validator, tapi bagaimana memastikan top 10 miner bukan orang yang sama pakai 10 akun beda? A) Pakai KYC (verifikasi identitas), jadi 1 orang = 1 akun maksimal B) Algoritma deteksi otomatis (tanpa KYC) C) Belum dipikirkan Kenapa penting: Kalau 1 orang bisa jadi 10 validator = dia kontrol sistem sendirian 8. DATA IDENTITAS Q: Kalau pakai KYC (verifikasi identitas dengan foto KTP dll), data itu disimpan dimana? A) Server pusat (Anda yang pegang) B) Perusahaan khusus KYC (seperti pihak ketiga) C) Enkripsi tersebar (tidak ada yang bisa buka kecuali algoritma) D) Belum dipikirkan Kenapa penting: Kalau data bocor = semua orang identitasnya ketahuan 9. HARGA EMAS (Untuk Hitung Nishob) Q: Algoritma perlu tahu harga emas real-time, dari mana dapat datanya? A) Dari satu sumber saja (misalnya website tertentu) B) Dari banyak sumber, terus di-rata-rata C) Belum dipikirkan Kenapa penting: Kalau dari satu sumber = bisa dimanipulasi 10. RATIO F-POINT DAN D-POINT Q: Kalau orang bakar 1 koin, dapat berapa F-Point dan D-Point? Contoh sederhana: Bakar 1 koin â†’ Pemilik dapat 10 F-Point Burner habis 10 F-Point untuk bakar â†’ Burner dapat 10 D-Point Atau belum ditentukan angkanya? Kenapa penting: Kalau ratio salah = sistem tidak seimbang (orang tidak mau bakar, atau semua orang cuma mau bakar) CARA JAWAB YANG MUDAH: Anda cukup bilang: "Pertanyaan 1: Jawaban A" (atau B, C, D) "Pertanyaan 2: Belum tahu" "Pertanyaan 3: Kira-kira 100,000 koin per event" dst... Repeat every event Why It Works: Nishob checked on annual haul completion Mining eligibility checked on snapshot during event Time window gap = exploit opportunity Impact: Wealthy users escape obligation systematically System loses funding (Baitul Maal depleted) Minnow support collapses Legitimacy crisis Severity: ğŸ”´ CRITICAL (9/10) Mitigation: Solution 1: Historical Holdings Check â”œâ”€ Mining eligibility requires: â”‚ â”œâ”€ Current holdings â‰¥ threshold AND â”‚ â””â”€ 30-day average holdings â‰¥ 80% threshold â”œâ”€ Prevent temporary borrowing â””â”€ Borrowed koin don't count toward eligibility Solution 2: Obligation Lock â”œâ”€ If holdings ever exceeded nishob in past 12 months: â”‚ â””â”€ Obligation flag = TRUE (cannot escape) â”œâ”€ Must fulfill obligation before mining â””â”€ Retroactive tracking Solution 3: Stake Requirement â”œâ”€ To mine: Must stake koin for duration of event â”œâ”€ Staked koin locked (cannot borrow & return) â””â”€ Unlock after event + 7 days Recommended: Combination of Solution 1 + 2 (Historical check + Obligation flag) E-2: Nishob Threshold Manipulation ğŸ”´ CRITICAL Attack Vector: Gold Price Oracle Attack: 1. Baitul Maal funding collapse Impact: System funding destroyed Minnow support disappears Economic model broken Trust collapse Severity: ğŸ”´ CRITICAL (10/10) Mitigation: Multi-Layer Oracle Defense: Layer 1: Multiple Oracles â”œâ”€ Minimum 7 independent sources â”œâ”€ Median calculation (not average) â”œâ”€ Remove outliers (top/bottom 15%) â””â”€ At least 5/7 must agree within 5% range Layer 2: Circuit Breaker â”œâ”€ Max change per day: Â±5% â”œâ”€ Max change per week: Â±15% â”œâ”€ Extreme changes trigger manual review â””â”€ Pause nishob update if suspicious Layer 3: Time-Weighted Average (TWAP) â”œâ”€ Use 7-day TWAP for nishob calculation â”œâ”€ Smooth out flash crashes â”œâ”€ Require sustained price change â””â”€ Prevent short-term manipulation Layer 4: Fallback Mechanism â”œâ”€ If oracle disagreement > threshold: â”‚ â””â”€ Use last known good value â”œâ”€ Alert validators for manual review â””â”€ Community governance intervention Layer 5: Oracle Reputation System â”œâ”€ Track historical accuracy â”œâ”€ Penalize bad actors â”œâ”€ Rotate low-reputation sources â””â”€ Incentivize honest reporting Recommended: ALL 5 layers (defense-in-depth) E-3: Burn-Mine Cycle Arbitrage ğŸŸ  HIGH Attack Vector: Event Timing Exploitation: 1. Target Harga Koin Q: Kira-kira Anda targetkan harga koin ini berapa saat launch? Contoh: $0.10 per koin? $1 per koin? $10 per koin? Belum ada target (biar market tentukan)? Contoh: 7 validator (minimal BFT) 10 validator (Anda sebut "top miners") 21 validator (seperti EOS) Belum ditentukan Kenapa penting: Untuk hitung keamanan (butuh berapa validator jahat untuk attack) A3. Minimum Stake untuk Validator Q: Apakah validator harus "stake" (kunci) koin sebagai jaminan? Ya, harus stake (berapa koin?) Tidak perlu stake (cukup rajin aja) Belum diputuskan Kenapa penting: Stake = pencegah validator jahat (kalau jahat, stake hilang) A4. Event Minimum Cooldown Q: Setelah satu event selesai, minimal berapa lama sampai event berikutnya bisa dimulai? Contoh: 12 jam (cepat, responsif) 24 jam (moderat) 3 hari (lambat, stabil) Tidak ada minimum (algoritma bebas trigger kapan saja) Kenapa penting: Prevent spam events, beri waktu user prepare A5. Contoh: Minimal 0.01 koin per transaksi Minimal 0.1 koin Tidak ada minimum (bisa kirim 0.00001 koin) Kenapa penting: Prevent dust spam (kirim jumlah tiny ribuan kali) B3. Account Creation Cost Q: Apakah bikin akun baru gratis atau ada cost? Gratis total (siapa saja bisa bikin) Perlu minimal deposit (misal: 1 koin untuk activate) Perlu referral dari user existing Belum diputuskan Kenapa penting: Prevent Sybil attack (satu orang bikin 10,000 akun) KATEGORI C: CONTRIBUTION SCORING DETAILS C1. Contribution Measurement Q: Waktu mining event, contribution diukur dari apa? Contribution Verification Q: Bagaimana algoritma tahu user beneran contribute, bukan fake/bohong? ğŸ‘ A3: ADAPTIVE STAKE REQUIREMENT âš ï¸ NEEDS DISCUSSION Anda bilang: "Stake disesuaikan kemampuan setiap orang" Ini ada trade-off: Pros (Advantages): âœ… Fair (poor people bisa jadi validator) âœ… Inclusive (tidak monopoli whale) Cons (Risks): âš ï¸ Whale stake 1000 koin, poor stake 10 koin â†’ Punishment tidak setara Kalau jahat, whale rugi 1000, poor rugi 10 Whale lebih berani cheat (loss lebih kecil relatif) âš ï¸ Sybil risk: Attacker bikin 100 akun "poor" (stake 10 each = 1000 total) Sama kayak 1 whale (1000), tapi lebih murah kalau kena slash Rekomendasi saya: OPTION A: Fixed Minimum + Reputation Multiplier â”œâ”€ Minimum stake: 1000 koin (fixed, everyone sama) â”œâ”€ Tapi: Poor people dapat "reputation boost" â”‚ â””â”€ Participation history, contribution record â”‚ â””â”€ Good actors dengan limited funds dapat priority â””â”€ Result: Fair tapi tetap secure OPTION B: Tiered Validator System â”œâ”€ Tier A Validators: Stake 5000 koin (high responsibility) â”‚ â””â”€ Validate large transactions, critical decisions â”œâ”€ Tier B Validators: Stake 1000 koin (medium) â”‚ â””â”€ Validate regular transactions â”œâ”€ Tier C Validators: Stake 500 koin (entry level) â”‚ â””â”€ Validate small transactions, less critical â””â”€ Result: Inclusive + matched risk-reward OPTION C: Bonded Insurance Pool â”œâ”€ Validators contribute to shared insurance pool â”œâ”€ Poor validator: Stake 500 koin + insurance coverage â”œâ”€ If fraud: Lose stake + banned from future â”œâ”€ Insurance pool compensate victims â””â”€ Result: Lower barrier, maintained security Mana yang lebih sesuai visi Anda? Atau ada ide lain? A4: BURNING EVENT COOLDOWN ğŸ”´ CRITICAL CONCERN Kekhawatiran Anda sangat valid! Scenario Anda: Event 1: Burning (supply turun 29M â†’ 27.5M) F-Point generated, D-Point consumed Event selesai â†’ F-Point RESET to 0 Urgent: Supply masih perlu turun lagi Event 2: Burning lagi (immediately) Problem: F-Point sudah di-reset! User tidak punya F-Point untuk participate Burning event GAGAL (tidak ada burner eligible) Ini DEADLOCK situation! ğŸš¨ SOLUSI yang saya usulkan: SOLUTION 1: Grace Period for Points â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ â”œâ”€ F-Point tidak reset immediately â”œâ”€ Reset rule: â”‚ â””â”€ IF next event = same type (burn-burn) â”‚ THEN: F-Point PERSIST (carry over) â”‚ â””â”€ IF next event = different type (burn-mine) â”‚ THEN: F-Point RESET as normal â”‚ â”œâ”€ D-Point same logic (persist if mine-mine) â””â”€ Result: Consecutive events tidak deadlock SOLUTION 2: Emergency Bootstrap Pool â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ â”œâ”€ Reserve pool: 5% dari Baitul Maal â”œâ”€ Used for: Emergency F/D-Point injection â”œâ”€ Trigger: IF consecutive event needed â”‚ â””â”€ Algorithm airdrop minimum F/D-Point â”‚ â””â”€ To top contributors (bootstrap participation) â”œâ”€ Paid back: Recipients must "repay" from future earnings â””â”€ Result: Always dapat kickstart event SOLUTION 3: Hybrid Cooldown â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ â”œâ”€ Normal cooldown: 24-48 hours (let points reset) â”œâ”€ Emergency cooldown: 0 hours (consecutive allowed) â”‚ â””â”€ BUT: Points persist (Solution 1) â”œâ”€ Algorithm decide: Normal vs Emergency â””â”€ Result: Flexible + Safe RECOMMENDED: Solution 1 + Solution 3 (Carry-over + Hybrid cooldown) Apakah ini solve kekhawatiran Anda? Jalan Tol Problem: Blockchain = jalan raya, macet kalau banyak mobil Solution: Bikin jalan tol (Layer 2) â”œâ”€ Jalan tol handle traffic harian (cepat, murah) â”œâ”€ Jalan raya (Layer 1) hanya handle blockchain) ğŸ”¹ SHARDING Analogi: Pecah Restoran Jadi Cabang Problem: 1 restoran, 1 dapur, 1000 customer = antri panjang Solution: Buka 10 cabang (shards) â”œâ”€ Each cabang handle 100 customer (parallel) â”œâ”€ 10x capacity â””â”€ Coordination: Central management ensure consistency Blockchain: â”œâ”€ Split network into 10 shards â”œâ”€ Each shard process different transactions (parallel) â”œâ”€ Beacon chain coordinate (ensure consistency) â””â”€ Result: 10x throughput ğŸ”¹ INCREASE BLOCK SIZE/SPEED Analogi: Perbesar Truk Pengiriman Current: Block every 5 seconds, 1000 TX per block = CRITICAL: Cannot launch without this CR-2: Wealth Evasion via Time-Based Gaming ğŸ”´ğŸ”´ Severity: 9/10 - SYSTEM INTEGRITY THREAT Masalah: Whale sophisticated bisa escape obligation dengan exploit time window: Whale Strategy (1-Year Cycle): Month 1-11: Hold 5,400 koin (just below 5,500 nishob) â”œâ”€ Status: NOT obligated âœ“ â””â”€ Avoid 2.5% contribution Month 12 (Mining Event): â”œâ”€ Borrow 10,000 koin from exchange/friend â”œâ”€ Total: 15,400 koin (temporarily) â”œâ”€ Mining dengan boosted holdings â”œâ”€ Earn maximum reward (whale advantage) â””â”€ Return 10,000 koin immediately after event Result: â”œâ”€ Get mining rewards (as if rich) â”œâ”€ Pay ZERO obligation (stay below nishob) â””â”€ Repeat forever Annual Profit Calculation: â”œâ”€ Mining rewards: ~500 koin (estimate) â”œâ”€ Obligation saved: 135 koin (5400 Ã— 2.5%) â”œâ”€ Total gain: 635 koin/year â”œâ”€ Cost: 0 (just borrow temporarily) â””â”€ ROI: INFINITE (pure profit, no cost) Why This Works: Obligation check = annual (haul = 1 year holdings) Mining eligibility = snapshot during event Time window gap = exploit opportunity No cross-checking between obligation status and mining participation Scale of Threat: IF 100 whales use this strategy: â”œâ”€ System loses: 13,500 koin/year in obligations â”œâ”€ Whales gain: 63,500 koin/year in unfair rewards â”œâ”€ Minnow support: CUT by 50%+ â””â”€ Legitimacy crisis: "System favors rich evaders" Real-World Parallel: Tax havens (offshore accounts timing) Flash loan attacks (borrow â†’ exploit â†’ return instantly) Wash trading (artificial volume for rewards) Solusi (Historical Holdings Requirements): SOLUTION 1: 30-Day Average Holdings Check â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ Mining Eligibility Requires: â”œâ”€ Current holdings â‰¥ threshold (already have this) â””â”€ 30-day average holdings â‰¥ 80% of threshold (NEW) Calculation: Average = (Day1_balance + Day2_balance + ... + Day30_balance) / 30 Example: User with 5,400 koin for 29 days, then borrow 10,000 for 1 day: â”œâ”€ Average = (5400Ã—29 + 15400Ã—1) / 30 = 5,733 koin â”œâ”€ This user CAN mine (average > threshold) âœ“ User with 100 koin for 29 days, then borrow 10,000 for 1 day: â”œâ”€ Average = (100Ã—29 + 10100Ã—1) / 30 = 433 koin â”œâ”€ This user CANNOT mine (average << threshold) âœ— â””â”€ Temporary borrowing detected! SOLUTION 2: Obligation Flag System â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ Retroactive Tracking: â”œâ”€ IF holdings EVER exceeded nishob in past 12 months: â”‚ â””â”€ Obligation flag = TRUE (sticky for 12 months) â”œâ”€ Mining requires: Obligation flag = FALSE OR already paid â””â”€ Cannot escape by moving coins temporarily Example: User A: Held 6,000 koin in Month 3 â”œâ”€ Obligation flag activated â”œâ”€ Even if transfers away â†’ flag remains â”œâ”€ Must pay 150 koin (6000 Ã— 2.5%) before mining â””â”€ Prevents evasion SOLUTION 3: Stake Locking for Mining â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ Mining Participation Requires: â”œâ”€ Lock (stake) coins for full event duration + 7 days â”œâ”€ Cannot borrow & return during event â”œâ”€ Locked amount must meet threshold â””â”€ Unlock only after event completely finished This makes borrowing useless: â”œâ”€ Borrow 10,000 koin â”œâ”€ Lock for event (7 days) â”œâ”€ Interest on loan >>>reward â””â”€ Not profitable anymore SOLUTION 4: Progressive Contribution â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ Instead of binary (pay or not pay): â”œâ”€ Holdings 0-2,000: 0% contribution â”œâ”€ Holdings 2,000-5,500: 1% contribution (scaled) â”œâ”€ Holdings 5,500+: 2.5% full contribution â””â”€ No "cliff" to game, smooth gradient Example: User with 5,400 koin: â”œâ”€ Under current system: 0 koin contribution â”œâ”€ Under progressive: ~120 koin contribution (2.2%) â””â”€ Still advantageous to have more, but can't fully evade Recommended Implementation: Primary: Solution 1 + Solution 2 (Average + Obligation flag) Secondary: Solution 3 (Stake locking) if needed Future: Solution 4 (Progressive system) for V2 Implementation Timeline: Critical: Must have before mainnet launch Development: 3-4 weeks Testing: 2 weeks (edge cases) Audit: Included in smart contract audit CR-3: Validator Cartel = System Capture ğŸ”´ğŸ”´ Severity: 9/10 - GOVERNANCE THREAT Masalah: Saya jelaskan ulang dengan BAHASA SANGAT SEDERHANA: CR-2: Orang Kaya Bisa Curang Sistem ğŸ”´ Masalah dalam bahasa awam: Si Budi (orang kaya): â”œâ”€ Punya 5,400 koin (hampir cukup untuk wajib bayar zakat) â”œâ”€ Batas wajib zakat: 5,500 koin â””â”€ Status: TIDAK wajib bayar (karena kurang 100 koin) Tapi Budi pintar: â”œâ”€ Waktu ada mining event (kesempatan dapat koin baru) â”œâ”€ Dia pinjam 10,000 koin dari teman â”œâ”€ Sekarang punya: 5,400 + 10,000 = 15,400 koin (sementara) â”œâ”€ Ikut mining dengan modal gede â”œâ”€ Dapat reward banyak (karena dianggap kaya) â”œâ”€ Setelah selesai: kembalikan pinjaman 10,000 koin â””â”€ Balik lagi ke 5,400 koin (tidak wajib bayar zakat) Hasil curang: âœ… Dapat reward mining (seperti orang kaya) âœ… TIDAK bayar zakat (seperti orang miskin) â””â”€ Budi untung 2x lipat! Sistem lihat koin Anda "30 hari terakhir rata-rata". Contoh Budi curang: â”œâ”€ 29 hari: punya 5,400 koin â”œâ”€ 1 hari: pinjam jadi 15,400 koin (waktu mining) â”œâ”€ Rata-rata 30 hari: (5,400Ã—29 + 15,400Ã—1) Ã· 30 = 5,733 koin â””â”€ Sistem: "Oke, rata-rata kamu cukup, boleh mining" Tapi kalau orang miskin coba curang: â”œâ”€ 29 hari: punya 100 koin â”œâ”€ 1 hari: pinjam jadi 10,100 koin â”œâ”€ Rata-rata: (100Ã—29 + 10,100Ã—1) Ã· 30 = 433 koin â””â”€ Sistem: "Rata-rata kamu rendah, TIDAK boleh mining" (Ketahuan pinjam sementara!)
